[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7764[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfi->rep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7765[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mcurlen = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfi->rep->representation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7766[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* curlen doesn't include the \[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m byte.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7767[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * XXX: If curlen + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m > ITEM_LABEL_LENGTH, we can't tell if[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7768[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * the representation has already been truncated [0m[1;39m([0m[39mof an up[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7769[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * to [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m byte UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m character[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or is just at the maximum [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7770[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * unless we search for [0m[32m" [0m[32m[[0m[32mtruncated[0m[32m][0m[32m"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich may not be[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7771[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * at the start.[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7772[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * It's safer to do nothing.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7773[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7774[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mITEM_LABEL_LENGTH > [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurlen + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7775[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mva_start[0m[1;39m([0m[39map, format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7776[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mstr = [0m[1;35mwmem_strdup_vprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mPNODE_POOL[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpi[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, format, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39map[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7777[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mva_end[0m[1;39m([0m[39map[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7778[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mWS_UTF_8_CHECK[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7779[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Keep fi->rep->value_pos *[0m[35m/[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7780[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mcurlen = [0m[1;35mws_label_strcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfi->rep->representation, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mITEM_LABEL_LENGTH, curlen, str, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7781[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcurlen >= ITEM_LABEL_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7782[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Uh oh, we don't have enough room.  Tell [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe user[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7783[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m * that the field is truncated.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7784[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7786[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7787[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mfi->rep->value_len = [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfi->rep->representation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - fi->rep->value_pos;[0m                               [2m                [0m
